–ø—Ä–∏–º–µ—Ä–Ω–æ —Ç–∞–∫:

@ $mol_mem
space_auto_create_if_empty() {
  if (!this.$.$mol_state_arg.value('space')) {
    const space = this.user().space_add()
    this.$.$mol_state_arg.value('space', space.land.id())
  }
}

auto() {

class m {
  @observable reset = []
  @observable arg = undefined

  @computed get val() {
    this.reset;
    if (this.arg) { const r = this.arg; this.arg = undefined; return r }
    return 1
  }
  set val(arg) { this.arg = arg }
}

m.val === 1
m.val = 2
m.val === 2
m.reset = []
m.val === 1

    @observable protected clientValue = undefined as string | undefined;
    @observable serverValue = ''
    @computed get value() {
        return this.clientValue ?? this.serverValue;
    }
    @action.bound protected onChange(value: string) {
        this.clientValue = value;

    @observable protected _state: State

    initial(): State {
        throw new Error('implement')
    }

    state(next?: State) {
        if (next !== undefined) this._state = next
        if (this._state === undefined) this._state = this.initial();
        return this._state;
    }
